Ias_Whtrns_Mst.Cc_Code
Select To_Char(Cc_Code)||'- '||Decode(
				  	           Nvl(Cc_A_Name,Cc_E_Name),
				  	           Nvl(Cc_E_Name,Cc_A_Name)) CC_name, To_Char(Cc_Code) 
				  	    From cost_centers 
							    Where c_s_m=(Select cc_type From cost_center_types 
							                  Where affected_by_trans=1)
							     And((
=1) Or
							         Exists(Select Cc_Code from privilege_cc 
							                 Where u_id=
							                  And Cc_Code=cost_centers.Cc_Code
							                  And nvl(Add_flag,0)=1
							                  And RowNum<=1)  )
						          Order By Cc_Code
Ias_Whtrns_Mst.Pj_No
Select To_Char(Pj_No)||'- '||Decode(
				  	           Nvl(Pj_A_Name,Pj_E_Name),
				  	           Nvl(Pj_E_Name,Pj_A_Name)) Pj_Name, To_Char(Pj_No) 
				  	    From Ias_Projects 
							    Where  Pj_Sub = 1
							     And((
=1) Or
							         Exists(Select Pj_No From Ias_Priv_Projects 
							                 Where u_id=
							                  And Pj_No=Ias_Projects.Pj_No
							                  And Nvl(Add_Flag,0)=1
							                  And RowNum<=1))
						          Order By Pj_No
Ias_Whtrns_Mst.Actv_No
Select To_Char(Actv_No)||'- '||Decode(
				  	           Nvl(Actv_A_Name,Actv_E_Name),
				  	           Nvl(Actv_E_Name,Actv_A_Name)) Actv_Name, To_Char(Actv_No) 
				  	    From Ias_Actvty 
							    Where  Actv_Sub = 1
							     And((
=1) Or
							         Exists(Select Actv_No From Ias_Priv_Actvty 
							                 Where U_Id=
							                  And Actv_No=Ias_Actvty.Actv_No
							                  And Nvl(Add_Flag,0)=1
							                  And RowNum<=1))
						          Order By Actv_No

KIT_ITEMS_DETAIL
select account.a_code a_code ,decode(:Parameter.Lang_dflt,1,A_Name,Nvl(A_Name_Eng,A_Name)) A_name,
decode(:Parameter.Lang_dflt,1,Group_Name,Group_E_Name) Group_Name
 from account,account_grouping,account_curr
Where
account.a_grouping=account_grouping.group_no(+)
And account.a_code = account_curr.a_code
And account_curr.A_CY=:Parameter.Stk_Cur
and Exists  ( Select Account_Type  From Account_Types  Where Nvl (Affected_By_Trans, 0) = 1
And Account_Type = account.a_s_m) 
and Exists (select 1 from priv_acc where u_id=:Parameter.user_no and a_code=account.a_code 
And a_cy =account_curr.a_cy 
and add_flag=1 and RowNum<=1)
And account.a_code Like Decode(:ias_whtrns_mst.tr_a_code,Null,'%',:ias_whtrns_mst.tr_a_code||'%')
order by account.a_code 
Select warehouse_details.w_code, 
       Decode(:Parameter.Lang_dflt,1,w_name,nvl(w_e_name,w_name)) w_name
from warehouse_details
where Exists (select 1 from PRIVILEGE_WH
where u_id=:Parameter.user_no and w_code=warehouse_details.w_code and add_flag=1 and RowNum<=1)
And Conn_Brn_No=Nvl(:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.Brn_No,Conn_Brn_No)
order by warehouse_details.w_code
Select warehouse_details.w_code, 
       Decode(:Parameter.Lang_dflt,1,w_name,nvl(w_e_name,w_name)) w_name
From warehouse_details
 Where Exists (Select privilege_wh.w_code
                             From privilege_wh 
                              Where privilege_wh.w_code = warehouse_details.w_code
                               And Nvl(Trnsfr_Wcode_Flg,0)=1
                               And u_id=:parameter.user_no
                               And RowNum<=1 )
order by warehouse_details.w_code
Select warehouse_details.w_code, 
       Decode(:Parameter.Lang_dflt,1,w_name,nvl(w_e_name,w_name)) w_name
From warehouse_details
Where Exists (Select privilege_wh.w_code
                             From privilege_wh 
                              Where privilege_wh.w_code = warehouse_details.w_code
                               And Nvl(Trnsfr_Wcode_Flg,0)=1
                               And u_id=:parameter.user_no
                               And RowNum<=1 )
/*Exists (  Select 1 From Ias_Items_Activity_Priv
                 Where Ias_Items_Activity_Priv.Activity_No = warehouse_details.Activity_No
                  And U_Id      = :Parameter.User_No
                  And Add_Flag  = 1
                  And RowNum   <= 1 )
order by warehouse_details.w_code
Select warehouse_details.w_code, 
       Decode(:Parameter.Lang_dflt,1,w_name,nvl(w_e_name,w_name)) w_name ,avl_qty
from warehouse_details ,Ias_Itm_Wcode
where Ias_Itm_Wcode.w_code = warehouse_details .w_code
 And i_code = :ias_whtrns_dtl.i_code
 And Exists (select 1 from privilege_wh
where u_id=:Parameter.user_no and w_code=warehouse_details.w_code and add_flag=1 and RowNum<=1)
order by warehouse_details.w_code
Select out_req_type ,
           out_req_no,
           out_req_date,
           w_code      , 
           doc_desc ,
           out_req_Ser,
           Use_Req_More_Once ,
           Brn_No            
From ias_out_request_mst
  Where Exists ( Select 1
                  From Request_types
                   Where request_types.out_trnsfr In (2,3) 
                    And ias_out_request_mst.out_req_type = request_types.req_type
                    And (request_types.Tr_Type Is Null Or request_types.Tr_Type =:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.Tr_Type)
 And RowNum <=1 
And Exists (Select 1 From priv_req_type
             Where priv_req_type.req_type = Request_types.req_type
             And Nvl(Fill_Flag,0) = 1
             And RowNum <=1    ))
    And Nvl(processed,0) =0
    And Nvl(inactive,0)  =0 
    And Nvl(approved,0)  =1 
And W_Code = Nvl(:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.T_W_Code,W_Code)
And Decode (Nvl(:Parameter.Chk_Wcode_Req_In_Whtrns,0),0, Nvl(:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.T_W_Code   ,0),1,F_W_Code) 
     = Decode (Nvl(:Parameter.Chk_Wcode_Req_In_Whtrns,0),0, Nvl(:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.T_W_Code   ,0),1,:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.W_Code)
Order By out_req_type,
         out_req_no
Select out_req_type ,
           out_req_no,
           out_req_date,
           w_code      , 
           doc_desc ,
           out_req_Ser,
           Brn_No ,
           Use_Req_More_Once
From ias_out_request_mst
  Where Exists ( Select 1
                  From Request_types
                   Where request_types.out_trnsfr In (2,3) 
                    And ias_out_request_mst.out_req_type = request_types.req_type
                    And (request_types.Tr_Type Is Null Or request_types.Tr_Type =:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.Tr_Type)
 And RowNum <=1 
And Exists (Select 1 From priv_req_type
             Where priv_req_type.req_type = Request_types.req_type
             And Nvl(Fill_flag,0) = 1
             And RowNum <=1    ))
    And Nvl(inactive,0)  =0 
    And Nvl(approved,0)  =1 
And W_Code = Nvl(:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.T_W_Code,W_Code)
And Decode (Nvl(:Parameter.Chk_Wcode_Req_In_Whtrns,0),0, Nvl(:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.T_W_Code   ,0),1,F_W_Code) 
     = Decode (Nvl(:Parameter.Chk_Wcode_Req_In_Whtrns,0),0,Decode(Nvl(:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.T_W_Code,0) ,0,0,W_Code),1,:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.W_Code)
And Decode(Nvl(:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.T_W_Code,0),0,0,W_COde) = Nvl(:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.T_W_Code,0)
Order By out_req_type,
         out_req_no

SELECT   Bill_date,
         Nvl(Si_A_Name,Si_E_Name) t_name, 
         Bill_no,
         c_name, 
         Ias_BIll_Mst.bill_doc_type bill_doc_type, 
         Cc_Code,
         Ias_BIll_Mst.w_code, 
         Bill_ser,
         Ias_BIll_Mst.Brn_No
    FROM Ias_BIll_Mst ,Ias_Sales_Types
     Where Ias_BIll_Mst.Si_Type = Ias_Sales_Types.Si_Type 
     And Exists (Select 1 From Ias_Bill_dtl 
                  Where Ias_Bill_mst.Bill_No  = Ias_BIll_dtl.Bill_NO
                    And Ias_Bill_mst.Bill_Ser = Ias_BIll_dtl.Bill_Ser
                    And Ias_Bill_dtl.W_Code   = :Ias_Whtrns_Mst.T_W_Code
                    And Rownum <=1)
     And Nvl (Ias_BIll_Mst.Stand_By, 0) = 0
 AND 1 = (CASE WHEN :PARAMETER.USER_VIEW_DOC_ENTR = 0 THEN 1
           ELSE (SELECT 1
                   FROM IAS_SHW_DOC_PRIV
                  WHERE U_ID = :PARAMETER.USER_NO
                    AND T_U_ID = IAS_BILL_MST.AD_U_ID
                    AND NVL (PRIV_FLAG, 0) = 1
                    AND ROWNUM <= 1)END)
AND (:PARAMETER.USER_NO = 1
    OR EXISTS (SELECT S_TYPE
                 FROM IAS_PRIV_AR
                WHERE U_ID = :PARAMETER.USER_NO
                  AND IAS_PRIV_AR.AR_TYPE = 3
                  AND IAS_PRIV_AR.S_TYPE = IAS_BILL_MST.SI_TYPE
                  AND NVL (VIEW_FLAG, 0) = 1
                  AND ROWNUM <= 1))
AND ((:PARAMETER.USER_NO = 1)
    OR EXISTS (SELECT 1
                 FROM S_BRN_USR_PRIV
                WHERE U_ID = :PARAMETER.USER_NO
                  AND S_BRN_USR_PRIV.BRN_NO = IAS_BILL_MST.BRN_NO
                  AND NVL (ADD_FLAG, 1) = 1
                  AND ROWNUM <= 1))
     AND Ias_BIll_Mst.Bill_No LIKE
            DECODE (:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.Doc_No,
                    NULL, '%',
                    :Ias_Whtrns_Mst.Doc_No || '%')
ORDER BY Bill_Date, Bill_No, Ias_BIll_Mst.Bill_Doc_Type
/*SELECT   Bill_date,
         Nvl(Si_A_Name,Si_E_Name) t_name, 
         Bill_no,
         c_name, 
         Ias_BIll_Mst.bill_doc_type bill_doc_type, 
         Cc_Code,
         w_code, 
         Bill_ser,
         Ias_BIll_Mst.Brn_No
    FROM Ias_BIll_Mst ,Ias_Sales_Types
     Where Ias_BIll_Mst.Si_Type = Ias_Sales_Types.Si_Type 
     And Nvl (Ias_BIll_Mst.W_Code, 0)  = Decode (:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.T_W_Code,Null,Nvl (Ias_BIll_Mst.W_Code, 0),:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.T_W_Code)
     And Nvl (Ias_BIll_Mst.Stand_By, 0) = 0
     AND Ias_BIll_Mst.Bill_No LIKE
            DECODE (:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.Doc_No,
                    NULL, '%',
                    :Ias_Whtrns_Mst.Doc_No || '%')

        From ias_whtrns_mst
         Where  ias_whtrns_mst.tr_inout_type = 1 
           And  Exists ( Select 1 
                          From priv_trnsfr_type
                           Where priv_trnsfr_type.tr_type =ias_whtrns_mst.tr_type
                            And Nvl(add_flag,1) =1
                            And  u_id   = :parameter.user_no

                    Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No                            
                     And privilege_wh.W_Code = ias_whtrns_mst.W_Code
	             And Nvl(Add_Flag,1) = 1 
	             And Rownum <=1 ))
            And 1 = (Case When :Parameter.User_View_Doc_Entr=0 Then
              1
            Else
           (Select 1 
              From Ias_Shw_Doc_Priv 
             Where U_Id =:Parameter.User_No
               And T_U_Id=ias_whtrns_mst.Ad_U_Id
               And Nvl(Priv_Flag,0)=1
               And Rownum<=1) End)
           And Nvl(tr_post,0) = 0
    And ((:Parameter.User_No=1)

                    Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No                            
                     And S_Brn_Usr_Priv.Brn_No = ias_whtrns_mst.Brn_No
	             And Nvl(Add_Flag,1) = 1 
	             And Rownum <=1 ))

Select 
(Nvl(Sum(in_out*(Nvl(p_qty,0)+Nvl(pf_qty,0)) ),0) /Nvl( :ias_whtrns_dtl.p_size,1)) avlqty 
From item_movement 
 Where I_code      = :ias_whtrns_dtl.I_code 
   And w_code      = Nvl(:ias_whtrns_mst.w_code,:ias_whtrns_dtl.w_code)
  And  expire_date = Nvl(:ias_whtrns_dtl.expiredate,'01/01/1900')
  And  batch_no = Nvl(:ias_whtrns_dtl.batchno,'0')
Having  (Nvl(Sum(in_out*(Nvl(p_qty,0)+Nvl(pf_qty,0)) ),0)/Nvl(:ias_whtrns_dtl.P_Size,1)) >0
AVLQTY
RG_BCHQTY_OLD
Select    
  Decode( batch_no,'0','', batch_no) batch_no,
(Nvl(Sum(in_out*(Nvl(p_qty,0)+Nvl(pf_qty,0)) ),0) /Nvl( :ias_whtrns_dtl.p_size,1)) avlqty 
From item_movement
 Where I_Code  =:ias_whtrns_dtl.I_code 
  And  w_code = Nvl(:ias_whtrns_mst.w_code,:ias_whtrns_dtl.w_code)
  And  expire_date= Nvl(:ias_whtrns_dtl.expiredate,'01/01/1900')
  And  batch_no Like  :ias_whtrns_dtl.batchno ||'%'
 Group By batch_no
   Having 
 (Nvl(Sum(in_out*(Nvl(p_qty,0)+Nvl(pf_qty,0)) ),0) /Nvl(:ias_whtrns_dtl.p_size,1))  > 0
BATCH_NO

Select  Decode(batch_no,'0','', batch_no) batch_no,
Decode( expire_date ,'01/01/1900','',expire_date) expire_date,
(Nvl(Sum(in_out*(Nvl(p_qty,0)+Nvl(pf_qty,0)) ),0) /Nvl( :ias_whtrns_dtl.p_size,1)) avlqty 
  From  item_movement 
    Where I_Code = :ias_whtrns_dtl.I_Code
    And   w_code =Nvl(:ias_whtrns_mst.w_code,:ias_whtrns_dtl.w_code)
  Group By batch_no,expire_date
Having (Nvl(Sum(in_out*(Nvl(p_qty,0)+Nvl(pf_qty,0)) ),0) /Nvl( :ias_whtrns_dtl.p_size,1)) >0

    Where I_Code = :ias_whtrns_dtl.I_Code

Select  w_code ,  
       Decode(expire_date,'01/01/1900','',expire_date) expire_date , 
       Decode(batch_no ,'0','',batch_no) batch_no ,
(Nvl(Sum(in_out*(Nvl(p_qty,0)+Nvl(pf_qty,0)) ),0) /Nvl( :ias_whtrns_dtl.p_size,1)) avlqty  
 From item_movement
  Where I_Code = :ias_whtrns_dtl.I_Code 
   And Exists ( Select 1 From Privilege_wh
                      Where Privilege_wh.w_code = item_movement.w_code
                        And add_flag =1

                        And RowNum <=1 )

RG_C_CODE
Select Customer.C_Code,
       Decode (:Parameter.Lang_dflt,1, Nvl (C_A_Name, C_E_Name),
                Nvl (C_E_Name, C_A_Name)) C_Name, 
       Decode (:Parameter.Lang_dflt,1, Nvl (C_Group_A_Name, C_Group_E_Name),
                Nvl (C_Group_E_Name, C_Group_A_Name)) C_Group_Name,
       NULL C_Class_Name
  From Customer,Customer_Group
 Where 
     Customer.C_Group_Code = Customer_Group.C_Group_Code(+) 
 And ((:Parameter.User_No = 1)
        Or (((:Parameter.Aralt = 1)
          And Exists (
                   Select 1
                     From Priv_Acc
                    Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
                      And A_Code = Customer.C_A_Code
                      And Nvl(Add_Flag,0) = 1 
                      And RowNum <=1 ))
 Or ((:Parameter.Aralt = 2)
            And Exists (
                   Select 1
                     From Ias_Priv_Customer
                    Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
                      And C_Code = Customer.C_Code
                      And Nvl(Add_Flag,0) = 1
                      And RowNum <=1 ))))
Order By Lpad(C_Code,30,'0')

Select M.I_Code, Nvl(M.I_Name,M.I_E_Name) I_Name,M.I_E_Name I_E_Name,
         D.Itm_Unt,   
       0 Avl_Qty,
0 I_Price,
         M.I_Desc,
         M.Vndr_I_Code
    From Ias_Itm_Mst M,Ias_Itm_Dtl D 
   Where M.I_Code=D.I_Code
     And Get_Items_Activity(M.Activity_No, :Parameter.User_No, :Parameter.Conn_Itm_Act_By_Usr_Priv, 1) = 1
     And (:Parameter.User_No=1 Or Exists(
            Select 1
              From Privilege_Gc
             Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
               And G_Code = M.G_Code
               And Nvl(Add_Flag, 0) = 1
               And Rownum <= 1))
     And (   (Nvl(M.Service_Itm, 0) = 1)
          Or Exists(
                Select 1
                  From Ias_Itm_Wcode
                 Where I_Code = M.I_Code
                   And W_Code = Nvl(:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.W_Code, W_Code)
                   And Nvl(Avl_Qty, 0) > 0
                   And Rownum <= 1))
          And Decode(:Parameter.P_Ord_Lov,
                2, Upper(M.I_Code||M.I_Name||M.I_E_Name||M.I_Desc||M.I_F_Desc),
                3,Upper(M.I_Code||M.I_Name),
                M.I_Code) Like
            Decode(:Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.I_Code,
                   Null, '%',
                   '%'|| Decode(:Parameter.P_Ord_Lov,2,Replace(:Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.I_Code,' ','%'),:Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.I_Code) || '%')
Order By Decode(:Parameter.P_Ord_Lov,
                2,Upper(I_Code || M.I_Name),
                M.I_Code),D.LVL_UNIT

RG_I_CODE_NO_POS
Select M.I_Code, Nvl(M.I_Name,M.I_E_Name) I_Name,M.I_E_Name I_E_Name,
         D.Itm_Unt,   
       Round(Decode(:Parameter.User_No,
                      1, Get_Icode_Avlqty(M.I_Code, D.P_Size, :Ias_Whtrns_Mst.W_Code),
                      Get_Icode_Avlqty_Priv(M.I_Code, D.P_Size, :Ias_Whtrns_Mst.W_Code,
                                            :Parameter.User_No)),
               :Parameter.No_Of_Decimal) Avl_Qty,
  0 I_Price,
         M.I_Desc,
         M.Vndr_I_Code
    From Ias_Itm_Mst M,Ias_Itm_Dtl D 
   Where M.I_Code=D.I_Code
     And Get_Items_Activity(M.Activity_No, :Parameter.User_No, :Parameter.Conn_Itm_Act_By_Usr_Priv, 1) = 1
     And (:Parameter.User_No=1 Or Exists(
            Select 1
              From Privilege_Gc
             Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
               And G_Code = M.G_Code
               And Nvl(Add_Flag, 0) = 1
               And Rownum <= 1))
     And (   (Nvl(M.Service_Itm, 0) = 1)
          Or Exists(
                Select 1
                  From Ias_Itm_Wcode
                 Where I_Code = M.I_Code
                   And W_Code = Nvl(:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.W_Code, W_Code)
                   And Nvl(Avl_Qty, 0) > 0
                   And Rownum <= 1))
          And Decode(:Parameter.P_Ord_Lov,
                2, Upper(M.I_Code||M.I_Name||M.I_E_Name||M.I_Desc||M.I_F_Desc),
                3,Upper(M.I_Code||M.I_Name),
                M.I_Code) Like
            Decode(:Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.I_Code,
                   Null, '%',
                   '%'|| Decode(:Parameter.P_Ord_Lov,2,Replace(:Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.I_Code,' ','%'),:Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.I_Code) || '%')
Order By Decode(:Parameter.P_Ord_Lov,
                2,Upper(I_Code || M.I_Name),
                M.I_Code),D.LVL_UNIT
I_CODE
I_NAME

         D.Itm_Unt, 
         null Avl_Qty,
         null I_Price,

         M.Vndr_I_Code
    From Ias_Itm_Mst M,Ias_Itm_Dtl D 
   Where M.I_Code=D.I_Code
     And Nvl(D.Main_Unit,0)=1
     And Get_Items_Activity(M.Activity_No, :Parameter.User_No, :Parameter.Conn_Itm_Act_By_Usr_Priv, 1) = 1
     And (:Parameter.User_No=1 Or Exists(
            Select 1
              From Privilege_Gc
             Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
               And G_Code = M.G_Code
               And Nvl(Add_Flag, 0) = 1

RG_ITM_UNT_AVLQTY
SELECT   D.ITM_UNT,
         ROUND(DECODE(:PARAMETER.USER_NO,1,
               GET_ICODE_AVLQTY (M.I_CODE,D.P_SIZE,:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.W_CODE), 
               GET_ICODE_AVLQTY_PRIV (M.I_CODE,D.P_SIZE,:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.W_CODE,
               :PARAMETER.USER_NO)),:PARAMETER.NO_OF_DECIMAL) AVL_QTY ,
         Lvl_Unit,
         P_Size
    FROM IAS_ITM_MST M,IAS_ITM_DTL D 
   WHERE M.I_Code=D.I_Code
     AND D.I_Code = :Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.I_Code
ORDER BY Lvl_Unit

RG_BATCH_DESC1
Select  A.Batch_Desc_No Batch_D_No1,A.Batch_Desc_Name Batch_D_Name1 ,
        A.Batch_Desc_No Batch_No ,Sum (In_Out * (Nvl(P_Qty,0)+Nvl(Pf_Qty,0)))/Nvl(:Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.P_Size,1) Qty         
   From 
(Select Batch_Desc_No,Nvl(Batch_Desc_A_Name,Batch_Desc_E_Name) Batch_Desc_Name From Ias_Batch_No_Contents Where Col_No=1 ) A, Item_Movement
   Where A.Batch_Desc_No=Item_Movement.Batch_No   
     And I_Code = :Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.I_Code
     And W_Code = Nvl(:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.W_Code, :Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.W_Code)
     And Expire_Date = Nvl(:Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.Expiredate,'01/01/1900')
     And Batch_No Like :Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.Batchno||'%'
Group By A.Batch_Desc_No ,A.Batch_Desc_Name ,
        A.Batch_Desc_No
Having Nvl(Sum(In_Out*(Nvl(P_Qty,0)+Nvl(Pf_Qty,0))),0)/Nvl(:Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.P_Size,1)>0
BATCH_D_NO1
BATCH_D_NAME1
BATCH_NO
RG_BATCH_DESC2
Select  A.Batch_Desc_No Batch_D_No1,A.Batch_Desc_Name Batch_D_Name1,
        B.Batch_Desc_No Batch_D_No2,B.Batch_Desc_Name Batch_D_Name2 ,
        A.Batch_Desc_No||B.Batch_Desc_No Batch_No ,Sum (In_Out * (Nvl(P_Qty,0)+Nvl(Pf_Qty,0)))/Nvl(:Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.P_Size,1) Qty         
   From 
(Select Batch_Desc_No,Nvl(Batch_Desc_A_Name,Batch_Desc_E_Name) Batch_Desc_Name From Ias_Batch_No_Contents Where Col_No=1 ) A,
(Select Batch_Desc_No,Nvl(Batch_Desc_A_Name,Batch_Desc_E_Name) Batch_Desc_Name From Ias_Batch_No_Contents Where Col_No=2 ) B, Item_Movement
   Where A.Batch_Desc_No||B.Batch_Desc_No=Item_Movement.Batch_No   
     And I_Code = :Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.I_Code
     And W_Code = Nvl(:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.W_Code, :Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.W_Code)
     And Expire_Date = Nvl(:Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.Expiredate,'01/01/1900')
     And Batch_No Like :Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.Batchno||'%'
Group By A.Batch_Desc_No ,A.Batch_Desc_Name ,
        B.Batch_Desc_No ,B.Batch_Desc_Name  ,
        A.Batch_Desc_No||B.Batch_Desc_No
Having Nvl(Sum(In_Out*(Nvl(P_Qty,0)+Nvl(Pf_Qty,0))),0)/Nvl(:Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.P_Size,1)>0
         
BATCH_D_NO1

        B.Batch_Desc_No Batch_D_No2,B.Batch_Desc_Name Batch_D_Name2,
        C.Batch_Desc_No Batch_D_No3,C.Batch_Desc_Name Batch_D_Name3 ,
        A.Batch_Desc_No||B.Batch_Desc_No||C.Batch_Desc_No Batch_No ,Sum (In_Out * (Nvl(P_Qty,0)+Nvl(Pf_Qty,0)))/Nvl(:Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.P_Size,1) Qty         
   From

(Select Batch_Desc_No,Nvl(Batch_Desc_A_Name,Batch_Desc_E_Name) Batch_Desc_Name From Ias_Batch_No_Contents Where Col_No=3 ) C , Item_Movement
   Where A.Batch_Desc_No||B.Batch_Desc_No||C.Batch_Desc_No=Item_Movement.Batch_No   
     And I_Code = :Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.I_Code
     And W_Code = Nvl(:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.W_Code, :Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.W_Code)
     And Expire_Date = Nvl(:Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.Expiredate,'01/01/1900')
     And Batch_No Like :Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.Batchno||'%'
Group By A.Batch_Desc_No ,A.Batch_Desc_Name ,
        B.Batch_Desc_No ,B.Batch_Desc_Name ,
        C.Batch_Desc_No ,C.Batch_Desc_Name  ,
        A.Batch_Desc_No||B.Batch_Desc_No||C.Batch_Desc_No
Having Nvl(Sum(In_Out*(Nvl(P_Qty,0)+Nvl(Pf_Qty,0))),0)/Nvl(:Ias_Whtrns_Dtl.P_Size,1)>0

Select Tr_No     ,
       Tr_Type,
       W_Code    ,
       tr_date   ,
       ref_no    ,
       Tr_Desc   ,
       F_Tr_Ser  ,
       Tr_ser    ,
       Brn_No
  From Ias_Whtrns_Mst
    Where W_Code=:Ias_Whtrns_mst.W_Code
And F_W_Code = :Ias_Whtrns_mst.T_W_Code
And Nvl(Rtn_Tr,0) = 0  
And Tr_InOut_Type = 2   
And ((:Parameter.User_No=1) Or Exists(Select 1 From Priv_Trnsfr_Type Prv
            Where U_Id=:Parameter.User_No 
              And Nvl(Fill_Flag,0)=1 
              And Prv.Tr_Type= Ias_Whtrns_Mst.Tr_Type
              And Rownum<=1))   
And Exists ( Select 1 From privilege_wh
                   Where add_flag            = 1
                    And  u_id                = :Parameter.user_no
                    And  privilege_wh.w_code = Ias_Whtrns_Mst.w_code
                    And RowNum  <=1      ) 
    And 1 = (Case When :Parameter.User_View_Doc_Entr=0 Then
                               1
                           Else
                            (Select 1 
                              From Ias_Shw_Doc_Priv 
                               Where U_Id =:Parameter.User_No
                                And T_U_Id=Ias_Whtrns_Mst.Ad_U_Id
                                And Nvl(Priv_Flag,0)=1
                                And Rownum<=1) End)
 And ((:Parameter.User_No=1) 
        Or Exists (Select 1 From S_Brn_Usr_Priv
                    Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No                            
                     And S_Brn_Usr_Priv.Brn_No = Ias_Whtrns_Mst.Brn_No
                 And Nvl(Add_Flag,1) = 1 
                 And Rownum <=1 ))
 And Not Exists (
select 1 from Ias_Whtrns_dtl
where doc_type_ref=12
And Doc_Type_Ref_Dtl = 11  
And doc_ser_ref=Ias_Whtrns_Mst.Tr_ser
  And tr_inout_type=1
  And rownum<=1
Select Decode( expire_date ,'01/01/1900',To_Date(''),expire_date) Expire_Date,
       Round((Nvl(Sum(in_out*(Nvl(p_qty,0)+Nvl(pf_qty,0)) ),0) /Nvl(:Ias_Out_Request_Dtl.P_Size,1)),6)  Avl_Qty
From  item_movement
  Where I_code = :Ias_Out_Request_Dtl.I_code 
   And  w_code =  Nvl(:Ias_Out_Request_Mst.F_w_code,:Ias_Out_Request_Dtl.F_w_code)
   And  expire_date Like Decode(:Ias_Out_Request_Dtl.expire_date  ,to_date(''),'%',:Ias_Out_Request_Dtl.expire_date||'%')
   And  batch_no  Like Decode( :Ias_Out_Request_Dtl.batch_no ,Null,'%', :Ias_Out_Request_Dtl.batch_no||'%')
Group By  expire_date ,batch_no 
Having 
 (Nvl(Sum(in_out*(Nvl(p_qty,0)+Nvl(pf_qty,0)) ),0) /Nvl(:Ias_Out_Request_Dtl.P_Size,1)) > 0
Select Decode( batch_no,'0','', batch_no) Batch_No  , 
       Round((Nvl(Sum(in_out*(Nvl(p_qty,0)+Nvl(pf_qty,0)) ),0) /Nvl(:Ias_Out_Request_Dtl.P_Size,1)),6)  Avl_Qty
From  item_movement
  Where I_code = :Ias_Out_Request_Dtl.I_code 
   And  w_code =  Nvl(:Ias_Out_Request_Mst.F_w_code,:Ias_Out_Request_Dtl.F_w_code)
   And  expire_date Like Decode(:Ias_Out_Request_Dtl.expire_date  ,to_date(''),'%',:Ias_Out_Request_Dtl.expire_date||'%')
   And  batch_no  Like Decode( :Ias_Out_Request_Dtl.batch_no ,Null,'%', :Ias_Out_Request_Dtl.batch_no||'%')
Group By  expire_date ,batch_no 
Having 
 (Nvl(Sum(in_out*(Nvl(p_qty,0)+Nvl(pf_qty,0)) ),0) /Nvl(:Ias_Out_Request_Dtl.P_Size,1)) > 0
Select warehouse_details.w_code, 
       Decode(:Parameter.Lang_No,1,w_name,nvl(w_e_name,w_name)) w_name
From warehouse_details
order by warehouse_details.w_code
Select warehouse_details.w_code, 
       Decode(:Parameter.Lang_No,1,w_name,nvl(w_e_name,w_name)) w_name
From warehouse_details
Where Exists (  Select 1 From Ias_Items_Activity_Priv
                 Where Ias_Items_Activity_Priv.Activity_No = warehouse_details.Activity_No
                  And U_Id      = :Parameter.User_No
                  And Add_Flag  = 1
                  And RowNum   <= 1 )
order by warehouse_details.w_code
Select  MNG_Code,G_Code ,
 Decode(:Parameter.lang_no,1,Nvl(mng_a_name,mng_e_name)
                            ,Nvl(mng_e_name,mng_a_name)) Mng_Name  
   From  Ias_mainsub_grp_dtl
     Where mng_code Like '%'||:Adv_Options.temp_data||'%'
    Order  by mng_code
Select  Group_NO,
 Decode(:Parameter.lang_no,1,Nvl(Group_a_name,Group_e_name)
                            ,Nvl(Group_e_name,Group_a_name)) G_Name  
   From  IAS_ALTERNATIVE_GROUP
    Where group_no Like '%'||:Adv_Options.temp_data||'%'
     Order  by group_no
RG_ASSTANT_NO

 Decode(:Parameter.lang_no,1,Nvl(Assistant_A_Name,Assistant_E_Name)
                            ,Nvl(Assistant_E_Name,Assistant_A_Name)) G_Name  
   From  Ias_Assistant_Group
    Where Assistant_No Like '%'||:Adv_Options.temp_data||'%'
     Order  by Assistant_No

RG_ITEM_NAME
Select Decode (:Parameter.Lang_Dflt,1,Nvl(M.I_Name,M.I_E_Name),Nvl(M.I_E_Name,M.I_Name)) I_Name,
         M.I_Code,
         D.Itm_Unt,
         M.I_Desc,
         M.Vndr_I_Code
    From Ias_Itm_Mst M,Ias_Itm_Dtl D
   Where M.I_Code=D.I_Code
     And Nvl(D.Main_Unit,0)=1
     And Nvl (M.Service_Itm, 0) = 0
         And Exists
                (Select 1
                   From Privilege_Gc
                  Where     U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
                        And G_Code = M.G_Code
                        And Add_Flag = 1
                        And Rownum <= 1)
         And Get_Items_Activity (M.Activity_No,
                                 :Parameter.User_No,
                                 :Parameter.Conn_Itm_Act_By_Usr_Priv) = 1
         And Decode (:Parameter.Lang_No, 1, M.I_Name, M.I_E_Name) Like
                Decode (:Paramtrs.Item_Name,
                        Null, '%',
                        '%' || :Paramtrs.Item_Name || '%')
Order By Decode (:Parameter.Lang_No, 1, M.I_Name, M.I_E_Name), M.I_Code

SELECT   order_date,
         order_no,
         c_name, 
         bill_doc_type, 
         Cc_Code,
         w_code, 
         order_ser,
         Sales_Order.Brn_No
    FROM Sales_Order
   WHERE  NVL (Sales_Order.Approved, 0) = 1
     AND NVL (External_Post, 0) = 0
     AND Sales_Order.Order_No LIKE
            DECODE (:IAS_OUT_REQUEST_MST.Doc_No_Ref,
                    NULL, '%',
                    :IAS_OUT_REQUEST_MST.Doc_No_Ref || '%')
     AND ((:Parameter.User_No=1) 
        Or Exists (select 1 From S_Brn_Usr_Priv
                    Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No                            
                     And S_Brn_Usr_Priv.Brn_No = Sales_Order.Brn_No
	             And Nvl(Add_Flag,1) = 1 
	             And RowNum <=1 ))
ORDER BY Order_Date, Order_No, Bill_Doc_Type

Select v_details.v_code,
       Decode (:Parameter.Lang_dflt,1, Nvl (v_a_name, v_e_name),
                Nvl (v_e_name, v_a_name)) v_name
  From v_details
 Where ((:Parameter.User_No = 1)
        Or (((:Parameter.Apalt = 1)
          And Exists (
                   Select 1
                     From Priv_Acc
                    Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
                      And A_Code = v_details.v_a_code
                      And Nvl(Add_Flag,0) = 1 
                      And RowNum <=1 ))
 Or ((:Parameter.Apalt = 2)
            And Exists (
                   Select 1
                     From Ias_Priv_Vendor
                    Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
                      And v_code = v_details.v_code
                      And Nvl(Add_Flag,0) = 1
                      And RowNum <=1 ))))
And  v_code Like      Decode(:ADV_OPTIONS.v_code,Null,'%',:ADV_OPTIONS.v_code||'%')

select P_M.po_no,
       P_M.po_type,
       P_M.po_date,
       P_M.v_code,
       P_M.v_name ,
       P_M.cur_code,
       P_M.po_ser,
       P_M.brn_no 
from   P_order P_M , P_Order_Detail P_D
where  P_M.Po_No = P_D.Po_No
And P_M.Po_Ser = P_D.Po_Ser
And Nvl(P_M.approved,0) = 1
And Nvl(P_D.Canceled,0) = 0 
and    Exists (select 1 
                from IAS_PRIV_AP 
                where u_id=:Parameter.user_no 
                and AP_TYPE=2 
                and p_type=P_M.po_type 
                and add_flag=1 
                and RowNum<=1)
and P_M.Po_No like '%'||:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.Doc_No||'%'
 And ((:Parameter.User_No=1) 
        Or Exists (Select 1 From S_Brn_Usr_Priv
                    Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No                            
                     And S_Brn_Usr_Priv.Brn_No = P_M.Brn_No
                 And Nvl(Add_Flag,1) = 1 
                 And Rownum <=1 ))
order by P_M.po_no,P_M.po_date

RG_SR
SELECT   RT_BILL_DATE, FLG_DESC T_NAME, RT_BILL_NO, C_NAME, W_CODE, CC_CODE, RT_BILL_DOC_TYPE,
         CC_CODE, RT_BILL_SER, IAS_RT_BILL_MST.BRN_NO,
         DECODE(:PARAMETER.lang_No,1, NVL(SR_A_NAME, SR_E_NAME),NVL(SR_A_NAME, SR_E_NAME))  SR_NM,BILL_AMT
    FROM IAS_RT_BILL_MST, S_FLAGS, IAS_RT_SALES_TYPES
   WHERE IAS_RT_BILL_MST.RT_BILL_DOC_TYPE = S_FLAGS.FLG_VALUE
     AND S_FLAGS.FLG_CODE = 'TYPE_NAME'
     AND S_FLAGS.LANG_NO = :PARAMETER.LANG_NO
     And Nvl(IAS_RT_BILL_MST.W_Code,0) = decode( Nvl(IAS_RT_BILL_MST.W_Code,0) ,0,0,:Ias_Whtrns_Mst.W_Code)
     AND IAS_RT_BILL_MST.SR_TYPE = IAS_RT_SALES_TYPES.SR_TYPE
     AND 1 =
            (CASE
                WHEN :PARAMETER.USER_VIEW_DOC_ENTR = 0 THEN 1
                ELSE (SELECT 1
                        FROM IAS_SHW_DOC_PRIV
                       WHERE U_ID = :PARAMETER.USER_NO
                         AND T_U_ID = IAS_RT_BILL_MST.AD_U_ID
                         AND NVL(PRIV_FLAG, 0) = 1
                         AND ROWNUM <= 1)
             END)
     AND (   (:PARAMETER.USER_NO = 1)
          OR (EXISTS(
                 SELECT 1
                   FROM PRIVILEGE_WH
                  WHERE PRIVILEGE_WH.W_CODE = Nvl(IAS_RT_BILL_MST.W_CODE,PRIVILEGE_WH.W_CODE)
                    AND U_ID = :PARAMETER.USER_NO
                    AND view_FLAG = 1
                    AND ROWNUM <= 1)))
     AND (   (:PARAMETER.USER_NO = 1)
          OR EXISTS(
                SELECT 1
                  FROM S_BRN_USR_PRIV
                 WHERE U_ID = :PARAMETER.USER_NO
                   AND S_BRN_USR_PRIV.BRN_NO = IAS_RT_BILL_MST.BRN_NO
                   AND NVL(VIEW_FLAG, 1) = 1
                   AND ROWNUM <= 1))
ORDER BY W_CODE, RT_BILL_DATE desc, RT_BILL_NO desc
